#  [](/thread/106165-123-break-bacis)1.2.3. break bacis 

  * 

  * [#1](/thread/106165-123-break-bacis "Post Permalink")

  * First Post: Edited Sep 20, 2013 7:18pm  Sep 14, 2008 5:21am | Edited Sep 20, 2013 7:18pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar32833_30.gif) TEB63](teb63)

  * Joined Jan 2007 | Status: Trader | [5,864 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=32833)

Hi One and all  
(rules updated)  
  
This is a great system - the 1-2-3 - break system.  
I trade the eurusd on the 5 mins charts with 3 Ema 5,30,100.  
on other pairs I trade on the hour, 4 hour & day chart ( I trade mostly on the hour - and confirm with the day)  
  
The 30ema & 100ema act as trend & channel... and keep me trading on the right side (hopefully!?)  
ie green (30ema) over red (100ema) only in an up trend  
price cannot be between the green (30ema) over red (100ema), ever when I trade.  
price & the 5 ema (yellow) must be over or under the two Higher emas  
The 5ema acts like momentum and/or a bird dog - Again price MUST BE OVER the 5 ema in an up trend  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 11.gif
Size: 15 KB](/attachment/image/147861/thumbnail?d=1365550471)](/attachment/image/147861?d=1221335685)   

  
But these are only the bit player the real deal is the 1.2.3 break  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 22.gif
Size: 18 KB](/attachment/image/147862/thumbnail?d=1365550471)](/attachment/image/147862?d=1221335800)   

  
As all ways (in an up trend)  
The "100 fibb" (2 pips over) is the entery point  
The "0 Fibb" (2 pips below) is the SL  
***Target : the "400 fibb" (2 pips under) (4.236 fibb works great) RRR 3 to 1  
I do keep an eye out for the 50 & 100 points on the chart & will use them if they are close to fib as targets.  
  
I find on the 5 min chart you have lots of trades. You will have loss but I find I win well over 80%.  
  
Only trade then the 3 ema are stacked in the right other and price is in the right place to them.  
best if you have some angle on the 30 & 100 ema & its great if they are pulling a part  
ie. the 30ema is running away from the 100 ema  
*** its best when the 5 ema is coming of the channel from between the two.  
( see blue box below this is great set up)  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 33.gif
Size: 20 KB](/attachment/image/147863/thumbnail?d=1365550471)](/attachment/image/147863?d=1221336458)   

  
  
trade when you have volume & trust the "fibbs" they work  
it is really best to set and forget & leave the room and let price wonder to your target  
  
I use the Fractals to help with the 1.2.3 set-ups but you don't need them  
  
  
its that simple  
  
cheers  
The real TEB63![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

I forgot  
  
Its really easy to see **consolidation** patterns   
on the 5 min chart   
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 44.gif
Size: 27 KB](/attachment/image/147870/thumbnail?d=1365550471)](/attachment/image/147870?d=1221338766)   

  
  
Blue boxes are the the moves   
The Yellow is the **consolidation** patterns,   
its a rest before the next move.   
80-90% you will see price move like this.  
  
Use the "fibbs" the same way as in the past post  
its easy money.   
  
Cheers   
  
TEB![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

  * Edited 9:09pm  Sep 14, 2008 8:05pm | Edited 9:09pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar32833_30.gif) TEB63](teb63)

Hi Guys   
  
Here is an advance trade on this stsyem   
I sometimes use.  
  
I only use it when there is a very clear 1.2.3   
And a big big hump in price.   
  
I get in on the break of the organge line 4a  
you get more pips the waiting for 4b  
(the bigger the hump the more the pips)   
but you will have more losses as well...but you are also closer to the SL.   
Again its two or three pips over & I am in.  
not the close of the candle   
  
The big hump is what makes it worth the risk  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 88.gif
Size: 19 KB](/attachment/image/147962/thumbnail?d=1365550488)](/attachment/image/147962?d=1221390001)   

  
  
Cheers And bye for now   
  
  
TEB ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

Hi Teb,

Could you please suggest settings of EMAs, Fibs, SL, and TP levels for higher TFs like 4H, D1, & W1?

Alfa99  
  
  

> [Quoting TEB63](/thread/post/2217328#post2217328 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hi One and all  
>    
>  I have had a lot of people ask me which system I am trading.  
>  In fact I am trading only the 1-2-3 - break system  
>  I am trading it on the 5 mins charts with 3 Ema 5,30,100.  
>  I am only trading the Eur/Usd (rarely the Eur/yen)  
>    
>  The 30ema & 100ema act as trend & channel...  
>  and keep me trading on the right side (hopefully!?)  
>  ie green (30ema) over red (100ema) only in an up trend  
>  price & the 5 ema (yellow)   
>  cannot be between the two, ever when I trade.   
>    
>  The 5ema acts like momentum and/or a bird dog  
>  Again price MUST BE OVER the 5 ema in an up trend  
>    
>  But these are only the bit player the real deal is the 1.2.3 break  
>    
>  As all ways (in an up trend)  
>  the "100 fibb" (2 pips over) is the entery point  
>  the "0 Fibb" (2 pips below) is the SL   
>  the ""200 fibb" (2 pips below) is the 1st target   
>  (close 1/2 of your possition move SL up on the 2nd 1/2 to 0+2 pips)  
>  the "300 fibb"(2 pips below) is your 2nd target close it out   
>  I do keep an eye out for the 50 & 100 points on the chart  
>  and will use them if they are close as targets.   
>    
>  if you like you can have a 3rd lot to play with   
>  you can let it run & keep moving up the SL.  
>    
>  I find on the 5 min chart you have lots of trades.   
>  You will have loss but I find I win well over 80%.   
>    
>  Only trade then the 3 ema are stacked in the right other  
>  and price is in the right place to them.   
>  best if you have some angle on the 30 & 100 ema  
>  its great if they are pulling a part  
>  ie. the 30ema is running away from the 100 ema   
>  its best when the 5 ema is coming of the channel from between the two.  
>  ( see blue box below this is great set up)  
>    
>  trade when you have volume  
>  & trust the "fibbs" they work  
>  it is really best to set & leave the room  
>  Trust me you will make more money.   
>    
>  I use the Fractals to help with the 1.2.3 set-ups   
>  but you don't need them   
>  you can use a 1sma just as well   
>  or do it just by eye  
>    
>  its that simple  
>    
>  cheers   
>  The real TEB63![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)
> 
> Ignored

Do you look for some criteria, like draw the fib (in an uptrend) from the first swing low after the cross of one of the EMAs? Or something else?

I am playing with the filters   
on the 30 mins I am now using 5 & 40 EMS as a filters   
1\. 5ema is for Momentum on the 30 min & the 40ema for the 4 hour   
2\. 5,30 & 100ema on the 5 min must be stacked in order   
  
Then I look for the 1.2.3. break

  * [#68](/thread/post/2304912#post2304912 "Post Permalink")

  * Oct 26, 2008 9:36pm  Oct 26, 2008 9:36pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar32833_30.gif) TEB63](teb63)

  * Joined Jan 2007 | Status: Trader | [5,864 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=32833)

I have been playing with this set up on the 1 min this week & had a lot of fun the % of wins to losses is lower. But you get more trades   
emas are 5,25,100  
  
Below is a trade I did on the Pound ...counter trend... one min   
both targets hit  
  
I

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: aa.gif
Size: 38 KB](/attachment/image/161917/thumbnail?d=1365553249)](/attachment/image/161917?d=1225024550)   

  
  
1\. Is the 1st stop loss .. 4 pips below the 3 of the 1.2.3 system   
in fact I put it under the "00" that was close to the 3   
2\. Is the 1st target ...take 1/2 the pips & move up stop loss to 0+1 pip  
3\. I moved up my SL to the newer high low to lock in pips on the 2nd lot  
4\. 2nd Target... closed trade   
  
  
TEB![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

1\. news I don't trade with this system  
2\. 1.2.3 patterns are set up by the ema  
you see what is happening   
if they are stacked & space between them   
there might be a good move  
but if they get tight there will be a good move also  
80% of the time the same way as the trend before  
  
teb![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

Adros  
  
Add the Fibs to the chart - right click or ctrl b and open the objects list  
  
Find the object 'fibo', click edit, then 'add' in level 1 which is equal to = 100% - so put 100% in the discription and keep adding for the levels you want. It should then stay as the default Fib setting for future use  
  
Red

  * Oct 31, 2008 11:34am  Oct 31, 2008 11:34am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar32833_30.gif) TEB63](teb63)

  * Joined Jan 2007 | Status: Trader | [5,864 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=32833)

> [Quoting fxxx](/thread/post/2317091#post2317091 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> hi, Teb!  
>  best and simplest explanation of using 123 & Fibo system   
>    
>  why such MA settings - just from experience? what will be on higher TFs (hourly, daily)  
>  what you do with volumes?
> 
> Ignored

the 5ema is almost the same as the normal momentun   
so on the 5 min we use 5 ema as the base   
we want the 30 min time frame which is 30 ema  
and we want a higher time frame say 2 hours 120 ema (some times I use 100ema)   
  
day is 5ema base, 20ema for a week, 80 ema for a month  
  
1 min is 5ema , 5 mins is 25 ema , 20mins is 100 ema   
(150ema would be 30 mins & 75ema would be 15 mins if you like them better)  
  
1 hour is 5ema, 4 hour is 20 ema ,day is 120ema (sometimes I use 100 ema)  
etc  
  
teb![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

> 
> Disliked
> 
> The good setup is with the lila Fibo.
> 
> Ignored

  
I personally find the Fibbs I use better & simpler  
but if your work for you great.  
But it might get a little hard with two sets of fibbs running around the same thread.  
  
To win in the 4X you only need 1 set -up   
1\. A trend -- The 3 EMA  
2\. A tool -- The Fractals  
3\. A trigger -- 1.2.3 break  
4\. A target-- TEB Fibbs  
  
you are using a diff. set-up & that is likely ok  
but not the one I am using that is all.  
  
cheers   
  
TEB![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

  * [ G-Man](g-man)

  * | Joined Mar 2006  | Status: Trader | [423 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=7111)

Hi TEB,  
  
Not doing much trading with this yet but I like the format and am looking at possibilities. Have a couple of questions though.  
  
On the pdf you posted about 1-2-3's, the author clearly looks for major trend reversals with that pattern. With the 5 min chart that isn't going to happen but do you ever trade against the ema's? From what I have seen there are many more opportunities if you allow yourself to do so. Otherwise are you just using the 1-2-3 as an entry point into the trend defined by the ema's.  
  
Secondly, do you only use the swing points defined by the fractals as those valid for the 1-2-3 pattern? Again if you are more flexible there are many more.  
  
I'm not suggesting that you should make any changes but just trying to get an understanding of what you are looking at.  
  
Keep posting.  
  
G-Man

yes it was not a good day for this system the markets had no trend   
(a little at the start of theday & at the end)  
  
keep an eye on the eur/usd if its not trending likely nothing else will  
as that is where most of the money is.  
  
if this is the case you need to move to a Higher TF &/or higher EMA  
I moved to 200ema on the 4 hour/ hour/15 mins (WSS)  
  
also fridays are hard & mondays too  
  
monday morning people are setting the trend   
fridays afternoon people are taking money out   
  
A good times to loss money   
  
But anytime between 1pm & 7pm est is bad trading   
just too few people in the markets   
  
cheers   
  
TEB

It is always the same question ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
  
The FIBlines 0 100 200 300 mean only that their distance is [equidistant](http://dict.leo.org/ende?lp=ende&p=thMx..&search=equidistant).  
You can edit the Fibos in MT4 under FIBO properties / Levels with right mousebutton.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar47489_3.gif) cheelu](cheelu)

  * | Joined Sep 2007  | Status: Trader | [183 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=47489)

Hi Guys,  
  
I've developed an indicator to visually identify the 123 setup . This is version 1 and it includes whatever is my understanding of TEB's methodologies.  
  
It draws a line between point 1 and point 2 and another line between point 2 and point 3 . Also draws the entry line. The lines alternate between DASH and SOLID so as to not confuse two consequetive setups.  
  
EDIT: Found an issue where some long 123 setups not displayed. fixed it. 

Attached Image

![](/attachment/image/170641?d=1226896518)

looks fine... but put the 1 hour on as well   
  
put a 5 ems on it   
& look at the last hour candle and the one on now   
  
look at the RSI on the Hour make sure you are not over buy/sold  
or have the BIG "D" happening   
  
then put on the trade & your winning will be higher  
you don't need it but it helps.  
  
This is a great systen in a strong trend ... other wise you may get killed   
the market is not trending right now  
  
use the WWS I am

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar32833_30.gif) TEB63](teb63)

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: 123a.gif
Size: 57 KB](/attachment/image/171478/thumbnail?d=1365555271)](/attachment/image/171478?d=1227037985)   

  
  
  
1\. The white boxes show about the same area on both chart   
  
2\. The big black lines on the hour... you want going the same way... if not don't trade.  
  
3\. The RSI is not over bought/or sold   
  
4\. also as a conformation   
a.the rsi is raising  
b. Has punched over ther 50% .  
  
5\. it hard to tell here   
but you do want the candle & candle formations in the right way   
  
6\. price must be over the 5 (in fact it would)   
  
tebr ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f601.png?v=15.1)

so keep your stops tight

[quote=TEB63;2375696]That is trading its a # & % game  
  
Yes I know, but how to decide what is important and what not ?  
Do you remember all these things ?   
Or do you have a policy to say it is a trade or not ?  
  
On the first view your method has SL = Target1.  
  
For example for a long SL = 60 in GBPUSD:  
  
entry is 2 (break 123) + 4 (spread) and round number 40 away   
=> target1 = 40-6-4 = 30  
  
but SL is 60+2 = 62.  
  
That means that the target in average is much less then the stop.  
Is there any formular wich keeps you away from trading ?

  * | Joined Nov 2008  | Status: Trader | [51 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=85835)

Hi   
  
I wrote a skript, it helps to post charts.   
  
Do the following:  
1 Install the skript.  
2 Make a hotkey with leftclick onto the skript  
3 Place a fibo onto the chart  
4 Rename the Fibo into "teb"  
5 click the hotkey to start the skript  
  
What you get:  
You will get the colored lines as in my last post.  
You can change the lines because of round numbers etc.  
You can read the places of Entry, Stop, Target1, Target2 for your orders.  
Others as well can read the values onto your screenshots....  
  
After you installed it like above its only:  
1 move the fibo  
2 press the hotkey  
3 fun

  * [ kris](kris)

Hi,  
  
Eversince TEB said that he is using WSS more, this thread seems to be dead.   
  
I feel that this method is much safer than WSS. It has higher success rates for me. The WSS method is much harder. Because the price does not immediately re-cross the 200ema on the smaller TF. So it suffers high drawdowns at time.  
  
Correct me TEB, I am having difficulty with WSS. WSS may lead to a change of intermediate trend and as a result trades become losses. While this method works in strong trends. And we are only trading with the strong trends. 

{Promotion Removed}

Really? I use another system:  
  
It's a point system based on  
  
1\. The weekly, daily, 4 hour, 1 hour, 30min, 15 min and 5 min charts  
2\. I look at news, interest rates differences, cot, trend, swing, candles, how other markets are moving and a few other things.  
  
Hope that helps.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar147504_8.gif) dee50](dee50)

  * Joined Jul 2010 | Status: Retired | [3,621 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=147504)

EU +21 +10 +17 +4  
  
Thanks Teb, do not know how I missed this thread, must have been the full stops in the thread title, I searched for 123 so 1.2.3 did not show up.  
  
Nice 123 method to add to my arsenal of 123 methods. I did not follow your rules entirely, my apologies.  
  
First Trade. 123 short from strong resistance area 1.3550, my favorite 123, 2 lots, first target the 300 second target the 400 & BRN 1.3500, first target achieved moved stop to 200. Stopped out at 200.  
  
Second Trade. According to Tebs rules. Safe first target the BRN 1.3500 & 200, last swing down did not reach the BRN so this time the BRN most likely target, second target the 300 at 1.3480. First target achieved moved stop to intermediate Fib 123.8%, the 161% fib was to close to the price. The Pin Bar off support BRN 1.3500 should have told me to close all but I held on, got stopped at 123.8%.

Wowowoooo it worked great, I messed it up only that I did not know at first how to partially close an order (@200%), so I closed it all. Let this be my greatest concern.  
  
So the rules I use so far on M5:  
\- Trend: Alligator's teeth (3xEMA) in order, RSI-14 on the right side of 50, ADX-14>20  
\- Tool: At first, nothing, how do you exactly use Fractals?  
\- Trigger: 1-2-3  
\- Stop: under point 1, with 2% risk  
\- Target: close 50% at 200% (move SL to riskless), close rest at 350%  
  
What do you think? Is 2% reasonable, or do you use a different rule? 

\--I'm a demo newbie, please be cautious.

This is virtually identicle to my own system that I completed just this year. I was looking for a simpler way to trade that avoided having to check multiple time frames, C.O.T data, news reports etc to make discretionary decisions on direction and entry but kept me on the right side of the move and trading when momentum is present. Wish I had just read this thread when you first posted it.  
  
I use a 2;1 reward/risk instead of your fib targets and longer periods for the ma's but the entry method is the same as are the rules about between the ma's.

I did not trade these - but very clear trades on the eurcad  
2 trades  
purple lines - SL are the stops  
white lines - Entries (bars close over the green 30 ema then under the 5 ema)  
blue lines - 1st targets  
red 100 ema and 30 ema green - clearly down  
yellow ema - we see a clear retracement then break back down  
the RRR is a little small on both trades

There are 2 Types of 123-Setups:  
  
1\. with Trends  
2\. Reverse Setups  
  
In this Fall I saw a Reverse........  
  
There are 2 great Threads here on FF about 123-Systems:  
  
1\. 1.2.3. break bacis: [https://www.forexfactory.com/thread/...23-break-bacis](https://www.forexfactory.com/thread/106165-123-break-bacis)  
2\. How to use the 123 strategy effectively: [https://www.forexfactory.com/thread/...gy-effectively](https://www.forexfactory.com/thread/232466-how-to-use-the-123-strategy-effectively)  
  
There are 21+85=106 Pages here  
I love this both Threads  
  
There you find all Information about this 2 Setups...  
  
IMHO:  
for me the best Stuff in FF
